  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_4634a5ef-c6b4-4918-a80f-fdb056af72c9'
      });

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer1098575396192406405">If your inner wolf and your body react rather enthusiastically to a psychotic Alpha male who’s own wolf has a tendency to turn feral, it can’t be a good thing, can it? Entering into a bargain with him wouldn’t be good either. Unfortunately, Taryn Warner, a latent wolf shifter, doesn’t have many options open to her right now. Okay, she has no options. Basically it comes dow</span>
  <span id="freeText1098575396192406405" style="display:none">If your inner wolf and your body react rather enthusiastically to a psychotic Alpha male who’s own wolf has a tendency to turn feral, it can’t be a good thing, can it? Entering into a bargain with him wouldn’t be good either. Unfortunately, Taryn Warner, a latent wolf shifter, doesn’t have many options open to her right now. Okay, she has no options. Basically it comes down to whether she’ll do what it takes to escape the arranged mating with the sick SOB that her father set up. As the answer in this case is yes, it looks as though she’ll have to agree to Trey Coleman’s deal… she’ll have to mate with him instead. <br /><br />Having always disliked shifter politics, Trey Coleman hadn’t bothered trying to form alliances with other packs. Now that his uncle – a wolf with many alliances – means to take Trey’s territory and his pack, he has no option but to form some alliances of his own very quickly or he’ll be easily outnumbered in the upcoming battle. He figures that the easiest way to do that would be to mate with a female whose Alpha is powerful and influential. There’s only one problem with that – he would then be stuck with her, and the last thing Trey wants is a mate. When he hears of Taryn’s situation, he offers her a deal – if she falsely claims he’s her true mate and allows him to claim her, he’ll save her from her arranged mating and then let her leave after the battle with his uncle is over. <br /><br />Sounds like a pretty straightforward deal...but soon Taryn and Trey realize they got more than they bargained for. Their mating instincts to protect and possess are weighing on them, they crave each other’s touch and company, and their inner wolves don’t like it whenever they’re apart. Add in that they’ll have to deal with this for an entire three months until the day of the battle finally arrives, and they’ve got themselves a recipe for disaster – or maybe for something quite the opposite. <br /><br /><i><b>Warning</b>: This novel contains an extremely sarcastic Alpha female, a broody possessive Alpha male, bitter in-laws, voyeuristic enforcers, a whole lot of dirty talk, and steamy bedroom battles for dominance. <b>Reader Advisory:</b> This edition also contains a graphic ménage scene - not for the faint-hearted, which is no longer included in subsequent editions.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1098575396192406405" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

    <div id=buyButtonContainer class="uitext buttons buyableFeature u-marginTopXSmall u-paddingBottomXSmall u-bottomGrayBorder" data-book-id=13522957 >

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6611471345526464328"><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393191ra/756938.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>BEWARE!! THIS BOOK IS ORGASMIC!! DO NOT READ UNLESS YOU HAVE YOUR BOYFRIEND/GIRLFRIEND/VIBRATOR NEXT TO YOU AND READY TO BE RAVISHED!!<br/><br/><br/>My rating:</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393191ra/756939.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Well, I heard this was a hot book, saw some pretty great quotes too, but actually had no idea until I read it myself. And WOW. This was full of humor, sarcasm, swearing, dirty talk (Trey <a href='http://beta.photobucket.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380380814ra/737815.gif' alt=' photo 703126.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> ) hot and sometimes kinky sex, and with the notorious orgy scene!<br/><br/>End result:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393191ra/756940.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>The story</b><br/><br/>Taryn awakens in a strange bed, with no memory how she got there. She soon find</span>
  <span id="freeText6611471345526464328" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393191ra/756938.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>BEWARE!! THIS BOOK IS ORGASMIC!! DO NOT READ UNLESS YOU HAVE YOUR BOYFRIEND/GIRLFRIEND/VIBRATOR NEXT TO YOU AND READY TO BE RAVISHED!!<br><br><br>My rating:</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393191ra/756939.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Well, I heard this was a hot book, saw some pretty great quotes too, but actually had no idea until I read it myself. And WOW. This was full of humor, sarcasm, swearing, dirty talk (Trey <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380380814ra/737815.gif" alt=" photo 703126.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> ) hot and sometimes kinky sex, and with the notorious orgy scene!<br><br>End result:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393191ra/756940.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><b>The story</b><br><br>Taryn awakens in a strange bed, with no memory how she got there. She soon finds out that the alluring male scent from the bed belongs to Trey Coleman <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393191i/756941.gif" alt=" photo 378786.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>, an alpha of a wolf pack, feared by almost everyone. He proposes a deal; they should mate, at least make it look like they mated, and it would solve their problems <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393191ra/756942.gif" alt=" photo 356261.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>. Taryn's father is forcing her to mate with a sadistic bastard, and she has virtually no way of escaping him. Unless she accepts Trey. He, on the other hand, has a war coming. Banished from his pack after he rightfully took over the leadership, the new alpha, his uncle, wants to take over Trey's pack and territory, and he can't allow that. So, the best way for them is to "mate" and make it seem believable. Of course, soon they'll realise they don't need to act at all <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393191ra/756943.gif" alt=" photo 508428.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"The guy could be so tactless and impatient, so remote and unapproachable. He was unbalanced. He had shitty communication skills. He thought apologies went in the form of oral sex, and he could brood with the best of them."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><b>Trey</b><br><br>Dirty talk was invented for Trey Coleman. No, Trey Coleman invented dirty talk! The man is a master at it <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374026ra/727924.gif" alt=" photo 279453.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> . I'm not really such a fan of it, but here... Oh my. <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749188.gif" alt=" photo fansmiley.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

And no one and I mean no one talks to her the way you just did, understand me?”</b><br><br>Wow Feral Sins is a Fantastic Shifter book!!!! I love Suzanne Wright. She has a great talent of writing sexy, manly heroes and Kick ass, sassy heroine. This book had me from the start and I didn't want to put it down. Dayum this book is smokin' hot. Taryn is about to be forced by her ass of a father, to mate a evil Alpha from another pack, whom she wants nothing to do with. She has been trying to find a way out, and that way out comes in the form of another Alpha named Trey Coleman. Trey needs political allies, and Taryn's father has a ton. So he offers to pretend to be true mates and get her out of her mating with the other alpha in hopes that the mating will gain her dad as a ally. Trey has a reputation of being psycho. Not to mention her wolf is crazy about him and his scent. Can she trust Trey enough to mate him and will they both be able to fight their attraction to each other?<br><br><b>“Move you son of a -” Then abruptly he plunged a long finger inside her, addressing that aching emptiness, and she practically liquefied against the wall, moaning. “That’s it, baby, be still for me.” He kept his thrusts shallow and leisurely, licking his claiming mark and liking her answering tremor. “Feel good?” “It’s alright, I guess.” </b><br><br>Trey:<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/trey22_zpszwxuuivb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

Instead of becoming the Alpha as it should have been, he was banished. Some of the pack left with him. Forming a pack with him as Alpha. Trey is very serious, he has a ton of responsibilities on his shoulders. He doesn't know what love is and he doesn't do fun! I love how Taryn brought life to him. She showed him how to play and brings laughter into his life. She softens his rough edges and makes him think of other's feelings. I love that Trey shows Taryn that she is worth respect and love and not less because she is latent.<br><br><b>“I don’t want anyone else, baby. I just want to hear my Taryn telling me she wants me. She is a latent wolf so she is always being picked on and treated badly. She had to learn to fight and save herself. I loved her, she has a lot of spirit and spunk . The only thing I didn't really get in this book was the one time he let his bros (pack mates) in the bedroom with them for a little ménage sex scene. (P.S. There is a edited version out there that doesn't have the tag team action in it.) I mean I have read a few ménage books, and they were good, but I am not a sharer. I will say this the group sex scene was hott, really hott I just couldn't connect to it. <span id="freeTextContainer6898986997217395056"><b>5 STARS!!!</b><br/><i>Oh. My. God. </i><br/>I don’t even know where to start with this one...<br/>Saying that this book is ‘HOT’ is an understatement... <br/>This book has a wicked awesome, funny, and sarcastic female; a super dominate, possessive, and sexy as hell alpha male; and some very steamy scenes! And if you are like me, you will LOVE every second of reading it!!!<br/><br/>Here is our leading lady- Taryn<br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/6b69c70a-063c-4b0d-9423-4a808f33999d_zps52e0344d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Taryn Warner is in a pack where her father is the alpha. She is a healer, but she is also a latent wolf. Because of this, </span>

God. </i><br>I don’t even know where to start with this one...<br>Saying that this book is ‘HOT’ is an understatement... <br>This book has a wicked awesome, funny, and sarcastic female; a super dominate, possessive, and sexy as hell alpha male; and some very steamy scenes! And if you are like me, you will LOVE every second of reading it!!!<br><br>Here is our leading lady- Taryn<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/6b69c70a-063c-4b0d-9423-4a808f33999d_zps52e0344d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

She really doesn’t have much of a choice. Its either mate with him, or be a lone wolf. They will mate, she can get away from the ass that wants to mate her, and he can get her fathers alliance. Neither of them are looking for a mate, so it will be a temporary solution for the both of them.Its a win win, right? The problem is, when wolves mate- they don’t always know its fake. Trey and Taryn have a crazy attraction to one another. The more they are together, the more they bond with one another... or at least their wolves do. After spending a lot of time together, marking one another, their wolves start to crave each other. When Trey’s wolf goes feral, Taryn is the only one that can calm him. Taryn starts to become one of the pack. At least most of Trey’s pack accepts her. But there is someone causing trouble in the pack...<br><br>Okay. Now let me tell you why I loved the two main characters...<br><br><b>TARYN WARNER</b> <br>Taryn may be the most hilarious, sarcastic, bad ass heroines I have ever seen! </a><br><br>Loved Trey and Taryn’s relationship. They were both funny, alpha, stubborn... but they were great together! I was really happy with how things turned out in the end...<br><b>

    <blockquote>“Love is giving someone the power to completely destroy you, and hoping that they won’t” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/FeralSins-thewolves_zps4cef8ce9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

If you are looking for something hot, steamy, funny, and paranormal make this your next read! I would highly recommend it!!! <br><br>&lt;3<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/dda33858-f5e7-4885-84d4-7e5d7b9d1e3a_zps05d3b5a2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer6495037336432654553"><b>Update: February 2, 2014 <br/><br/>4 1/2 Stars for edited version</b><br/><br/>I increased my rating by a half star for the edited version of this story. It's amazing what proper editing can do for a book, and this one was already good. I'm also glad the out-of-place "orgy" scene was removed and replaced with a sex scene that felt more authentic to this couple's relationship. I forgot how much I loved this book. The editing made it even better! <br/><br/><b>Solid 4 stars for the unedited version</b><br/><br/>I was originally planning to wait unt</span>
  <span id="freeText6495037336432654553" style="display:none"><b>Update: February 2, 2014 <br /><br />4 1/2 Stars for edited version</b><br /><br />I increased my rating by a half star for the edited version of this story. It's amazing what proper editing can do for a book, and this one was already good. I'm also glad the out-of-place "orgy" scene was removed and replaced with a sex scene that felt more authentic to this couple's relationship. I forgot how much I loved this book. The editing made it even better! <br /><br /><b>Solid 4 stars for the unedited version</b><br /><br />I was originally planning to wait until the edited version of this book was released in February to start this story, as the book will under go professional editing with the somewhat infamous <b>
  <i>orgy</i>
</b> scene being removed. <br /><br />Well, what can I say for myself other than my <b>
  <i>curiosity</i>
</b> got the better of me (go figure!). Even though I have limited time, I had to find out what all the talk was about regarding the somewhat infamous and out-of-place scene I've recently heard so much about. <br /><br />I'll start out by saying I really enjoyed this book a lot. Although there were time I cringed at the explicitness of the content, I found <i>Feral Sins</i> to be a captivating, intriguing, and full-of-eroticism read. It sported wonderfully developed, fun, and witty characters and a paranormal world that was fascinating, easy to understand, and held my attention from start to finish. <br /><br />That said, I finally understand what all the <b>incredulity</b> was about and why many were truly <b>baffled</b> by this particular over-the-top and out-of-place sex scene. It's inclusion made absolutely and positively no sense in the overall plot. In fact, it detracted from it and made a <b>mockery</b> of the characters previous behaviors and feelings. Not to mention it was anything but erotic!<br /><br />Other than that, I very much enjoyed this book and can't wait to read the edited version. <br /><br /> </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1421331508" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3956458403017511883">The more books I read by Suzanne Wright, the bigger fan I become of her work. Her writing style is so unique, her witty dialogue is fantastic and the characters she creates come to life right off the pages. <br/>One of my GR friends suggested I read The Phoenix Pack – and so happy I followed her suggestion!!!<br/><br/>Feral Sins is the 1st book in The Phoenix Pack and what a fantastic read it was!!!<br/>It had a great storyline with engaging characters, scorching and sizzling scenes and some of the most unforgettab</span>
  <span id="freeText3956458403017511883" style="display:none">The more books I read by Suzanne Wright, the bigger fan I become of her work. Her writing style is so unique, her witty dialogue is fantastic and the characters she creates come to life right off the pages. <br>One of my GR friends suggested I read The Phoenix Pack – and so happy I followed her suggestion!!!<br><br>Feral Sins is the 1st book in The Phoenix Pack and what a fantastic read it was!!!<br>It had a great storyline with engaging characters, scorching and sizzling scenes and some of the most unforgettable and hilarious dialogue.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445379510i/16639705.jpg" alt=" photo img-thing201_zpsbnpevkim.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>Trey Coleman, alpha wolf shifter &amp; Taryn Warner, a dominant and latent wolf shifter (she can’t shift but her wolf is caged inside her) are the main characters in this book.<br><br>Taryn is desperate to get out of a mating that her father has arranged with someone that she’s determined not honor.<br><br>Trey needs to build alliances with the other packs and proposes that he and Taryn pretend to be mated so both will achieve what they want. And once the alliance with her father is finalized, they can both go their own ways. But what starts off purely as a contract, it soon becomes more complicated by the growing feelings they have for each other.<br><br>Trey is the kind of alpha you do not mess around with. Feared by other shifters for his strength and his extreme dominance, he rules his pack, which he has been the alpha of since the age of 14, when he was outcast by the pack after killing his father, with an iron fist.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445379510ra/16639706.gif" alt=" photo alpha_zpsijvl5tol.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>No one ever crosses him or is ever challenged except by one person….Taryn. She’s not the kind of person to bow down to anyone and she means anyone….never mind if it’s the pack’s alpha…….<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445379510i/16639707.jpg" alt=" photo tyler-hoechlin-batman-man-of-steel-casting-rumors_zpsaup7ohu8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>I absolutely adored Taryn. She’s fiery, takes sh@@$$#** from no-one and if provoked….<blockquote><b>“She was a sarcastic bitch and when she was pissed off the sarcasm took on a life of its own.”</b></blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445379510i/16639708.jpg" alt=" photo 03867a01269bded10b7a1c08b33240b6_zps98ae0aba.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I loved watching Trey and Taryn challenge each other – how both fought for dominance…..<blockquote><b>“When I fuck you Taryn-and make no mistake about it, baby, I will fuck you-the only talking you’ll be doing is begging me to let you come. And don’t doubt that I’ll make you come. Not just the once. You’ll come over and over again, until I decide you’ve had enough. Until I decide that I’ve had enough.”</b></blockquote>Yeah, right Trey….Taryn is just not giving in that easily…<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445379510i/16639709.jpg" alt=" photo e65cf9a3eebddce5129eb3885c64ca93_zpsda7zpggf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>And their connection was incredible and very touching. Discovering that the best thing in their lives was each other. Never mind that they had to go through a lot of obstacles and uncertainties and fears before realizing how much they felt for one another.<br><br>These two ooze sexual tension on a high scale….their sex scenes are hot and sizzling…<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445379510ra/16639710.gif" alt=" photo giphy_zpsr71vc4jb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Trey and Taryn really shone for me. I loved how their relationship developed – getting to knowing and understanding each other and accepting each other’s good and bad points…..it was a total and fabulous thing….<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445379510i/16639711.jpg" alt=" photo superthumb_zpsh92nagik.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>One of the most enjoyable parts was the interaction between Taryn and Greta, Trey’s grandmother. It made for the most hilarious scenes ever……and one of those was Greta giving Taryn a hard time about the fact that Trey had chosen her instead of one of the pack members…I laughed my head off…….<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445379510i/16639712.jpg" alt=" photo 46f524e2-e712-42c3-81d7-363f13ca4595_zps9udrttrd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Okay, so there’s steamy moments between Trey and Taryn….but when you had more than the two in one scene…yes, I ‘m talking about the ménage…no not a trois …..more like neuve…<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445379510ra/16639713.gif" alt=" photo vCWo1dI_zpszwlyycuq.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">….<br>.when the male Pack members join in the fun…….nothing like I was expecting…believe me…it’s scorching hot and no not seedy at all…..hell, those wolves sure know how to please a woman…can I please have Tao for myself!!!!!! <br><br>I am really excited to start book #2….can’t wait for what happens next!!!<br><br>Recommend this book……….A DEFINITE YES!!!!<br><br><b>One of favorite quotes :</b><br><blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445379510i/16639714.jpg" alt=" photo superthumb201_zpsecp6j8md.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote></span>

  <span id="freeText11297533803645920744" style="display:none"><br><b>✮ 4 SCORCHING HOT AND WOLFISH STARS. ✮</b><br><br><b>Damn, this book was on fire...and I LOVED IT!!!</b><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397739ra/767726.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>✦ Taryn Warner ✦--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397739i/767727._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>✧ Trey Coleman ✧--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397739i/767728._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397739i/767729.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~</b><br><br>I am so glad I FINALLY came around to reading <b>Feral Sins</b>. After reading so many raving reviews about this book, it seemed like an absolute MUST READ and to me it turned out to be one too. I loved Suzanne Wright's easy flowing writing style that brought me straight to La La Land where I was happy to stay during the amount of time it took me to read this gem. <br><br><br><b><u>THE STORY</u></b><br><br>At the beginning of the story we meet our heroine, Taryn, who is the daughter of a wolf pack leader, Lance. Taryn is a wolf shifter and a healer but because of her latency, she's never had a good relationship with her father, who considers her as weak. And now, Lance has decided it's time for Taryn to mate into another clan which is why he has set her up to be claimed by the alpha leader of the pack, a guy Taryn absolutely despises.<br><br>So, when Trey Coleman, the Alpha of the Phoenix Pack, offers her a way out of the arranged mating, it's either that or risking the chance of becoming a lone wolf. Trey himself is pretty much at war with his own uncle and in order too gain more allies, he proposes Taryn to become his "fake" true mate. That way, she gets out of the arranged claiming and he will get more forces if it ever were to come to an actual battle against his uncle. <br><br>They both agree to the temporary mating bond, but after a while it becomes clear that their temporary arrangement might have some much more permanent consequences...<br><br><b><u>✦ TARYN</u></b><br><br>Taryn is one hell of a kick-ass heroine!!! She has to be one of the most (if not <i>the most</i>) sarcastic characters I've ever come across... I loved her snarky attitude and the fact that she always stood up for herself and never cared what anyone else thought of her. <br><br><b><i>"Taryn, are you even listening to me?" <br>"I pretended to so let that be enough."</i></b><br><br>The banter between her and the other pack members (especially between her and Trey's grandmother Greta) was just hilarious! Still, it was kind of weird when she randomly started to curse like this at times:<br><br><b><i>"A motherfucking ass-licking sod of a cock-sucking goddamn bitch."</i></b><br><br>But I guess that's just part of her personality and it didn't really bother me that much. <br><br><b><u>✧ TREY</u></b><br><br><b><i>"He was kind of like the Black Mamba snake; fiercely aggressive, had a bad reputation, and was respected, admired and feared all at the same time."</i></b><br><br>Trey is the leader of the Phoenix Pack; he's powerful, strong, domineering and HOT as hell! All in all, he's the PERFECT Alpha Male. 'Nuff said.<br><br><b><i>"When I fuck you Taryn - and make no mistake about it, baby, I will fuck you - the only talking you'll be doing is begging me to let you come. And don't doubt that I'll make you come. Not just once. You'll come over and over again, until I decide you've had enough. Until I decide that I've had enough."</i></b><br><br><br><b><u>✦ TARYN + TREY ✧</u></b><br><br>Together they are like FIRE &amp; ICE. There's a lot of PUSH AND PULL that goes on between these two! Trey is an Alpha Male, Taryn is an Alpha Female, despite her being latent, and neither of them is willing to let the other "dominate" their relationship. But in the end, it was mostly Trey who dominanted the relationship (or maybe that's just what Taryn wanted him to believe).<br><br><b><i>"Now, who do you fucking belong to?"<br>After a slight hesitation she conceded with a snarl. "You"<br>"That's right, baby, and just in case you're ever tempted to forget..." He yanked her head back and bit down hard into the soft flesh of her neck where it would be visible for everyone to see.</i></b><br><br>And there was a lot more biting and scratching etc. after that...</p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397739ra/767730.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397739i/767731.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397739i/767732.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After a while, Trey and Taryn started to grow closer to each other and their mating bond became stronger and stronger. Everything was going pretty well actually and then, since I still had the old version of the book, there was suddenly the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the graphicly described ménage scene -- <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/548039.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn't really know what to think of it and my reaction constantly switched like this...</p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397739ra/767733.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The scene was actually pretty HAWT but in the context of the story it just didn't make much sense for Trey to be okay with that. He went from being overly protective and possessive and not allowing any of the other guys so much as being too close to her to well...being okay with <i>a lot</i> of guys touching her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Anayway, the new version of the book doesn't include this scene anymore so future readers won't have to worry about it. <br><br>Overall, this book was VERY ENTERTAINING and A LOT OF FUN to read with the perfect amount of sexy scenes and a great dose of humor and a HEA!!! Suzanne Wright, from now on, you are my new favorite PNR author to watch out for!!!<br><br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/339662.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>♡♥ <b><u>Favorite quotes</u></b> ♥♡<br><br><b><i>"Of course it was worth noting that she suffered from NRS Syndrome (Never Remembers Shit)"<br><br>***<br><br>"I quite like your blouse, Greta. Wouldn't you like to slip into something more comfortable, though? Perhaps a come?"<br><br>***<br><br>"Hey, I have a suggestion, why not put a condom over your head - if you're going to act like a complete dick then it makes sense to dress like one."<br><br>***<br><br>"Is there no way you could just pull your bottom lip over your head and swallow?"<br><br>***<br><br>"If your left leg is Thanksgiving, and your right leg is Christmas, can I visit you between the Holidays?"<br><br>***<br><br>"Love is giving someone the power to completely destroy you, and hoping that they won't."<br><br>***<br><br>"Just give me a second.   <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

      Read with Smut Monday Club

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=menage">menage</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=shifters-or-weres">shifters-or-weres</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer553021305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3809116217122689526"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>
      <s>Love is giving someone the</s>
    </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/>Actually, no. Forget the sweet book quote. That is not how my review should have started. Let's try again...<br/><a href='http://imgur.com/m0H42xq' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412185i/810489._SX540_.png' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>3.5 stars. Poor Shakespeare is rolling over in his grave right about now. Bear with me because I am asking this for a reason. Depending on when you purchased <i>Feral Sins</i>, you will either receive a copy of the orgy version, or the non-orgy version. If you purchase the book now, that scene will have been edited out.<br/><br/>I have the 'in all its g</span>
  <span id="freeText3809116217122689526" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>
      <s>Love is giving someone the</s>
    </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Actually, no. Forget the sweet book quote. That is not how my review should have started. Let's try again...<br><a href="http://imgur.com/m0H42xq" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412185i/810489._SX540_.png" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>3.5 stars. Poor Shakespeare is rolling over in his grave right about now. Bear with me because I am asking this for a reason. Depending on when you purchased <i>Feral Sins</i>, you will either receive a copy of the orgy version, or the non-orgy version. If you purchase the book now, that scene will have been edited out.<br><br>I have the 'in all its graphic glory' version. Yes, I was happy to have this copy because if I didn't have this copy, I would have been tormented to know what I'd missed out on and would have had to have gone to the author's website and read that scene anyway. My thoughts on the orgy scene are mixed, however. It was a hot scene, but I had a hard time matching it up in my mind with this story. I don't completely buy that it worked here, given the way Trey had been acting before. Someone else did a nice job of explaining why Trey was willing to share in that context and some excellent points were made but I personally didn't buy it.<br><br>Erotic books (or books with multiple sex scenes) are such a mixed bag for people. Often, it all boils down to what your kinks are. If a subject is touched upon in an erotic book which doesn't mesh well with what turns your crank, then there's a good chance you won't like it. And of course this would be completely understandable if you are one of those people who doesn't like the sexual gimmes that were being featured in this book.<br><blockquote>
  <b>But I'll give you one guess as to whose crank WAS getting turned.</b>
</blockquote><br>MEMEMEMEME...MEMEMEMEMEMEME...MEMEME...<br><br>Do I sound enthusiastic enough? Here's why :<br><br>~ Dominating, rough sex (in terms of biting, marking, etc. No BDSM)<br>~ Dirty talk (i.e. who owns this? who's going to take this?)<br>~ Exhibitionism! (hey, your fantasy may not be my fantasy)<br>~ Back-and-forth power struggles (i.e. woman reclaims what was taken and would do some marking of her own)<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He didn't want to change her, wasn't disregarding her own strength the way others had before him.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>All of my little sweet spots were hit. For those of you who've known me for a while, I have the book <i>Willing Victim</i> as one of my favorites for non-BDSM-type rough sex. I love power struggles in the bedroom. I love when a man says you're going to take it and the woman says hell no and fights him back and they both get all hot and bothered in the process until one person wins out. YUM. YUM. YUM.<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He knew she'd fight him like a wildcat.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>So again, if this type of sex doesn't get you going, you won't like this book. It's about mating and claiming and all of the primal urges that wolves (we're dealing with shifters here) feel for their mates. I love pack dynamics and alpha wolf with their mate dynamics. Within the confines of the story, it all works. <i>Because it's a paranormal story with so much being explained as instinctual</i>, it all works.<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Now, who do you fucking belong to?"<br>After a slight hesitation, she conceded with a snarl. "You."<br>"That's right, baby, and just in case you're ever tempted to forget..." He yanked her head back and bit down hard into the soft flesh of her neck where it would be visible for all to see.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Should I even talk about the plot? Was there even a plot? Yes, there actually was something resembling a plot. You might want to be forewarned that the plot and sex are about equal to each other in this book, so we're definitely working with an erotic book featuring a story, and not the other way around. Basically, we learn about some of the pack members and some of the conflicts between the Phoenix Pack and other packs. The shifters themselves were drawn in an interesting way, with the "inner wolf" having a huge and separate influence on the person as a whole. <br><br>Since I had the older copy, I did notice a few typos, but they were few and far between. I'm assuming there will be even less of this in the newer edition. I do have to go on record stating that I hated the use of terms such as <i>baby</i> and <i>hot little body</i>. I also could have done without Trey talking about wanting to pump his cum inside of Taryn. Bleh. Surprisingly, I was not bothered by Trey calling Taryn <i>his little bitch</i> or telling her that she was going to <i>take it like a good girl</i>. After all, they are wolves...<br><br>I do think the book was a touch too long. It wasn't a huge deal because I am a pro skimmer when I need to be, but with some editing and shortening, this could have been a solid 4 star book. <br><br>Other than the sex, my favorite part of <i>Feral Sins</i> was pretty much every scene between Greta (the alpha's grandmother) and Taryn. Watching these two women rip on each other was too darn funny. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Wouldn't you like to slip into something more comfortable, though? Perhaps a coma?"<br><br>"Oh sorry, I was just busy picturing a gag in your mouth."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>In the end, I found that I liked this book FAR better than I was expecting to. I got lucky and had all of my fun fetish buttons pushed. You may not feel the same way if you prefer something different with your erotic reads. So tread carefully and know what you want before you pick this book up. If you choose to go there, I hope you have as much fun as I did!<br></span>

  <span id="freeText5688314563546503224" style="display:none">Reread on July 24/ 2019!<br />I have been wanting to pick up this series again and finally finish it! This way I know I will be able to enjoy the series more because I will know all the little details!<br />I am glad to report that I enjoyed this instalment just as much as I did the first time I read it! I am very happy to be moving on to the second story now!<br /><br /><br />This was an awesome read!! I had a hard time putting this book down and I didn't want it to end!! It entertained me from beginning to end and I am already anxious for book #2 and hopes it comes out soon!!<br />Taryn is set to mate with a shifter she is not happy about. Her father has not given her a choice as she is a "latent" wolf (she can't shift fully into a wolf) therefore he feels she is not valuable to their pack. By mating with this shifter her father will gain an alliance that he wants. Trey comes into the picture and propositions Taryn with a deal where they will pretend they are "True mates" and that way no one can dispute her mating with Trey and not Roscoe. They will only have to play at being true mates for several weeks and then Taryn is welcome to go her own way. Of course, once Trey and Taryn spend time together they begin to bond for real and their feelings for one another deepen. She also begins to feel accepted by most of the pack members in Trey's pack and they being to highly respect Taryn as their Alpha Female. Taryn is a healer and when the pack witness her healing Trey their respect solidifies once they see her abiliby. Of course, not everyone is happy with this arrangement and conflict does arise and there is a traitor in the midst..<br />I have to say the one liner's that Taryn delivers in this book are hilarious! I highlighted almost every second page with funny one liners!! EG.."Hey, I have a suggestion, why not put a condom over your head- if your going to act like a complete dick then it makes sense to dress like one"! This is one of many one liners that come out of Taryn's mouth and for those alone they make this story so enjoyable! Luckily there is so much else that is good too. The sex is hot and steamy just the way I like it. There is some kink involved too, so your not just getting "vanilla" sex in this story, and what you do get will have you squirming in your chair for sure!<br />Even the other pack members are enjoyable and I look forward to getting to see them again in ther own stories! One of the members likes to deliver cheesy come on lines, and they are just as funny as Taryn's!<br />All in all, I highly recommend this book..For readers who love shifter romances this is a must read. I am very impressed for a self publised author and I will be checking out any other work that she has done.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5688314563546503224" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

If I were to bat for the other team, she will be on my list of fictional girlfriends. It was so refreshing to read about a heroine that isn't some virginal ingenue, stands up for herself, and has a sharp tongue and sarcastic tendencies. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“We should probably clear this up right now, psycho boy. I don’t have a submissive bone in my body, so don’t bark at me unless you’re happy to be ignored.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>She doesn't back down from anyone or anything and can deliver some of the best lines I have ever read.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I suppose this is the part where you enlighten me about how you’re his ex— perhaps even the love of his life— and then I’m supposed to feel insanely jealous. Sorry, but it’s just too early in the morning for me to muster that kind of response. Maybe you should try again later.” Though that wasn’t to say that Taryn wasn’t tempted to slap her purely for having touched Trey— as idiotic as that was. <br><br>“Seriously, Trey, you can’t honestly have mated her. She’s not even your type. I mean, she’s thin. And mouthy. And small. Even her boobs are on the small side.” <br><br>“I have nice feet.” <br><br>“You’re not his type!” <br><br>“You mean because I can read and write?”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>She is not some damsel in distress, she is Trey equal in every sense, and Alpha female. <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Oh. And what is it you think you’re going to do to me now?” <br><br>Mousy smirked. “I’m thinking that I’d like to fuck that mouth of yours.” <br><br>“Sorry. I was raised to never put small objects in my mouth or I might choke.”</blockquote>
</i><br><br>To top it off, she can kick some ass. Honestly, girl crush material!<br><br>The book also had some of the most creative curses I had ever read<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“You motherfucking, ass-licking, son of a goddamn cocksucking bitch!”</blockquote>
</i><br><br><br>It's an erotic romance, so the steam is off the charts. Suzanne Wright has a definite gift for writing a smoking hot love scene. Ladies, I'd warn you to have a few pairs of clean undies on hand when reading this they will be melted off.<br><br>It wasn't all just book porn; it had a great plot and many laugh out loud moments. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“And yet you haven’t thrown out your inherently evil grandmother.” <br><br>Chuckling, he shaped her waist with his hands. “I know she’s being a little difficult right now, but she’s one of those people who grow on you.” <br><br>“No, she’s one of those people who are like Slinkys.” <br><br>“Slinkys?”<br><br> “Yeah. Basically useless, but they make you smile when you push them down the stairs.”</blockquote>
</i><br><br>If you like your romances steamy, your heroines feisty and kick-ass, and your heroes Alpha, dirty-mouthed, and seriously sexy than this book is for you! <br><br>5 sexy stars from me<br><br> <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10190898193636279392" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

LOL!)<br/><br/><i>If you don't have a cold shower nearby, a significant other sleeping peacefully unaware beside you, if you have dog allergies or you are just prissy and can't handle sarcasm and wit, consider yourself warned!!!</i><br/><br/><b>5 HUGE Mindblowing stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395124ra/760892.gif' width='217' height='124' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I don't know what took me so long to start this book...   <b>WARNING</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395124i/760891.jpg" width="250" height="333" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>Contains TnT</b>
</i> (Trey &amp; Taryn, nicknamed, pantent pending! LOL!)<br><br><i>If you don't have a cold shower nearby, a significant other sleeping peacefully unaware beside you, if you have dog allergies or you are just prissy and can't handle sarcasm and wit, consider yourself warned!!!</i><br><br><b>5 HUGE Mindblowing stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395124ra/760892.gif" width="217" height="124" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I don't know what took me so long to start this book... I just needed a little nudge that all of you naughty girls provided me with!<br>To say I loved it, it doesn't do this book justice. It surprised me, it got me hot and bothered, it amused me, it shocked me (I'll come back to that later). Best damn shifter story, in league (in my opinion) to Singh's Changelings Series.<br><br>Taryn is a latent wolf and a healer in her father's pack. Her own father seems to despise her and she is forced to mate with an asshole alpha just to strengthen her father's alliances.<br><br>Trey became alpha of his father pack in the tender age of 14, when he killed him in a challenge, splitting the pack in two. He is closed off and a killing machine. His own uncle (who leads the other half of the pack) disputes his authority and wants the whole pack for himself.<br><br>The two of them agree to temporarily mate to solve their individual problems and the rest... Well the rest is an AMAZING book!<br><br><b>Taryn:</b>The girl deserves a medal! Funny by nature and sarcastic by choice this girl can kick your ass and make you laugh at the same time. A survivor, a keeper, a winner!<br><br><b>Trey:</b> aka Cujo. The alpha to end all alphas... Possesive, jealous, smart, psychotic, I absolutely loved him! And that foul mouth of his had me squirming in my seat!<br><br><b>The Pack:</b> Just like the annoying older siblings you can't help but adore!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395124i/760893._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="312" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Where can I join or is by invitation only??? Damn all the good ones are slipping though my fingers...<br><br><br>And here comes my one and only big objection.................<br>What was that???????????????????<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395124i/760894.jpg" width="530" height="398" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Come on seriously where did that come from? <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395124i/760895.png" width="300" height="222" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>It was like the book was abducted by aliens and they inserted the scene just to screw with our minds... The whole scene was totally out of character but I reluctantly admit, it was rather HAWT in an embarassing and entirely wrong way... well enough said!!!<br><br>I found out that the author plans a re-issue without this scene.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395124ra/760896.gif" width="387" height="251" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>THANK YOU!!!!! Go girl!! Yaaaaaaaaaayyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyy! The best decision you could ever make! Thank you for taking into consideration our feelings and really glad you are listening to your readers! You got me for life!!!<br><br><b>So, all of you, who go on with your lives, blissfully unaware of this book's existence, go READ it, like NOW!</b> </span>

<div id="review_524304895" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/524304895" />
    <a title="≿Jᴀᴅᴇ≾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2875809-j"><img alt="≿Jᴀᴅᴇ≾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594287090p2/2875809.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/524304895?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="≿Jᴀᴅᴇ≾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="≿Jᴀᴅᴇ≾" href="/user/show/2875809-j">≿Jᴀᴅᴇ≾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2875809-j?shelf=heavy-on-romance">heavy-on-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2875809-j?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2875809-j?shelf=adult-fiction">adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2875809-j?shelf=stopped-sequel">stopped-sequel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2875809-j?shelf=werewolves-shifters-rawr">werewolves-shifters-rawr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2875809-j?shelf=hate-it">hate-it</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer524304895" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15737639402738214098">After seeing the high rates and comments in Goodreads, I was so curious to see what was up with this book. So, after reading it... I had thrown my phone away, hugging myself, huddled at the empty corner of my room, promising myself that I would recover from this as I rocked back and forth.<br/><br/> I am so appalled, disgusted and mad at this book. -> Let’s go for a ride, shall we?<br/><br/> [But before we do that, why the heck is the two main character’s name is close? Taryn – Trey?] Okay, never-mind. Its not like</span>
  <span id="freeText15737639402738214098" style="display:none">After seeing the high rates and comments in Goodreads, I was so curious to see what was up with this book. So, after reading it... I had thrown my phone away, hugging myself, huddled at the empty corner of my room, promising myself that I would recover from this as I rocked back and forth.<br /><br /> I am so appalled, disgusted and mad at this book. -&gt; Let’s go for a ride, shall we?<br /><br /> [But before we do that, why the heck is the two main character’s name is close? Taryn – Trey?] Okay, never-mind. Its not like that's not impossible in real life, right?<br /><br /> Alrighty, the story started great, better than great actually. Taryn Warner WAS a great main character, with her quick wit and sarcastic comments that made me laugh out loud and seeing her standing up for herself and fight was another thing I admired. Trey Coleman WAS a respectable Alpha, which made all the fan girls swoon, he was the kind of bad boy that girls wished secretly to have before going to sleep. We HAD funny, realistic minor characters around us, some a little more far-distant and dull than others, but we had a few good ones. <br /><br /> There was a love and hate relationship at first, but it was more like love and lustlustustlust... and oh yeah, he is such an ass. But, who cares? right? Cause, you know… his hot and all, and Taryn is not dense or shallow or anything, it’s just that Trey doesn't know how to express himself. And it went like that on and on and on for a good chunk of the story. <br /><br /> Let’s talk about the plot a little, or maybe the lack of it. There was (had to be) a little plot (story structure) for the two couple to meet and when they did, BANG. There was no more plot, it was all about how Taryn felt or how Trey was acting, or why was he acting a certain way. It was all about them-them-them-them. There was no world outside, no one else existed, and we didn't even have a villain (Come on, all stories have one) until more than half way through the story.<br /><br /> No proper story other than two people describing how hot each other is and how they want to bang each other. Let’s just say, after reading these two bang each other more than I could count, I got bored. As the bored reader who progressed even further into this story, Taryn’s so called ‘witty-sarcastic-comebacks” was getting unbelievably lame. <br /><br /> “No need to take it out on me that you’re so wrinkled you have to screw your hat on.”<br /><br /> “We’re all going to calm down and drive back to Bedrock and you’re not going to give me any shit about it or so help me God I’ll beat you so bad you’ll have to put toothpaste in your ass to brush your teeth!”<br /><br /> Ha-ha. Wait-What? <br /><br /> So I’m almost done ranting, bear with me.<br /><br /> So the story is about to get wrapped up and be done with, when something absolutely crazy and sick happened, and it was at the very end of the book. Throughout the whole story we got to see Trey’s over-protectiveness-jealous personality, and there was no surprise there, he is a wolf and a pack leader. When one of the pack members starting ‘liking’ Taryn, we got to see Trey’s jealous strike, again and again.<br /><br /> “But Trey was honestly considering stabbing the wolf with his fork.” (I’m cutting them short and clean not to ruin anything I possibly don’t think is necessary.) <br /><br /> So, when a certain sex scene at the very end came up, not only was it unnecessary and absolutely useless, it was mortifying to read. I felt like clawing my eyes out and forget I read that part or maybe the whole story, but unfortunately, it wasn't that easy. Trust me, I tried.<br /><br /> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There was an orgy scene with pack members. WHAT...WHAT THE FUCK?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /> How? How can you put that in the story? Or maybe I should say- Why? How in that logic mind of yours did that scene make any sense to anything we just read? It was like a fucking slap to the reader’s face. What happened to our not-so- submissive girl? Or our respectable, over-protectiveness, and jealous pack leader?<br /><br /> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ What’s more horrifying is that Taryn’s unborn baby is going to grow up around the pack members and that includes all the guys who she gave blowjobs to. Disturbing fact.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I read somewhere there is another version, the ending edited in a different way. Ugh, wish I read that one. I had no fucking clue! And its too late... the horror.<br /><br /> This story had so much room for improvement, our main character was a damn healer, and we did not see much of her skills throughout the book and that was so freaking sad. <br /><br />ps: A guy calling his mate ‘bitch’ in bed is such a great way to ruin the whole mood. I honestly thought our main character, Taryn, would have more respect for herself.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15737639402738214098" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2206725082" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6023687882123315548">Theres shapeshifters and then theres SHAPESHIFTERSSSS <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1539357698ra/26439623.gif' width='170' height='160' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1577311480ra/28668486.gif' width='170' height='160' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>This was an AWESOME wolf romance that I thoroughly enjoyed wayyy 2 much. <b>And sure the cover looks like an <u>8th grader's attempt at a collage</u></b> with all the elements copied and pasted next to each other but it gets the message of the book across so I'll allow it<br/><br/><b>Taryn</b> is a wolf but struggles to actually transform. But that doesn't stop her from being a total kickass sassy heroine who honestly has some of the greatest witty liners I have ever read</span>
  <span id="freeText6023687882123315548" style="display:none">Theres shapeshifters and then theres SHAPESHIFTERSSSS <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1539357698ra/26439623.gif" width="170" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1577311480ra/28668486.gif" width="170" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This was an AWESOME wolf romance that I thoroughly enjoyed wayyy 2 much. <b>And sure the cover looks like an <u>8th grader's attempt at a collage</u></b> with all the elements copied and pasted next to each other but it gets the message of the book across so I'll allow it<br><br><b>Taryn</b> is a wolf but struggles to actually transform. But that doesn't stop her from being a total kickass sassy heroine who honestly has some of the greatest witty liners I have ever read <br><blockquote>
<b><i>“Hey, I have a suggestion, why not put a condom over your head – if you’re going to act like a complete dick then it makes sense to dress like one.”</i></b> </blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1604342870ra/30325364.gif" width="170" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1604342870ra/30325365.gif" width="170" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I was gawking while reading this book and actually started cry- laughing so hard my roommates were CONCERNED for my mental being<br><br>Our love interest, <b>Trey</b> is a sexy, <b>dirty</b> talking, fighting alpha who honestly might be little crazy ... but we aint even mad about that <br><br>This book was pipping hot, I'm talking steam pouring outta each page <br><blockquote>
<b><i>“Move you son of a -” <br>Then abruptly he plunged a long finger inside her, addressing that aching emptiness, and she practically liquefied against the wall, moaning. <br>“That’s it, baby, be still for me.” He kept his thrusts shallow and leisurely, licking his claiming mark and liking her answering tremor. “Feel good?”<br>“It’s alright, I guess.”</i></b> </blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1604342870ra/30325366.gif" width="170" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The characters were dynamic, both great in their own unique personalities and their chemistry when they are together. Honestly they the kinda characters I would read their POV in a longer more adventure type book. I guess I just have the settle for the hot erotica, bummer man <br><br>If you like werewolves, read this book<br>if you like sass, read this book<br>if you like tough alphas that are sweet to their mates, read this book<br>JUST READ THE GODDAMN BOOK<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454937429ra/18031337.gif" width="170" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>A lotta the time, you go searching for wolf books and its very much a hit or miss. <br><br>I hate it when the girl is a baby wimp and the guy is a total jerk whose only redeeming qualities is his large penis <i>*gag*</i> (yes that was a sex joke on multiple layers) <br><br>But this book really balanced the plot, and tensi0n between our characters without making either one cringey.... Also Trey had some cute vulnerable moments that had me wooing and sighing like I was in a goddamn Jane Austin novel <br><br><b>
  <i>“I’d never purposely hurt you. Never. I’m a man, which means I’ll fuck up. Regularly. I’m not good with words, I spout crap when I’m angry, <u>and I’m about as romantic as a pebble.</u> But…See, I’m not good with words. All I can say is you’re important to me ”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449489594ra/17291985.gif" width="170" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Critiques? <br><br>I guess it kinda short and I honestly could've kept reading for a longer more plot driven novel <br><br>it was just hot as fuck with wolves, of course I loved it don'tttt judge meeee</span>

<div id="review_736043053" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/736043053" />
    <a title="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea"><img alt="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1390412715p2/3258936.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/736043053?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

</b>- 5 plus stars<br><br><br><b>★Review★</b><br><br>You know when you read a book that is so perfectly satisfyingly good your soul just sighs.....?<br><br>Well, that was this book.<br><br>To say I loved it is an understatement.<br><br>I adored the heroine, I made so many notes on my kindle of her dialogue. She is by far one of my favourite ever, if not THE favourite heroine ever. She was funny, strong and just downright awesome.<br><br>And Trey was almost as equally as awesome. And together - sublime.<br><br>I loved the world the author has developed here, and how she has made seem fresh a quite frankly overdone genre.<br><br>Taryn and Trey both had their own issues and vulnerabilities to overcome, and their story to a HEA is not easy at times. But it was an exciting read, and there was not one moment where I skipped ahead or my attention was lost.<br><br>This book is hot, funny, exciting and above all made me happy.<br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11394613828614507058">I've been in a book-slump for while now, with every book I read or started either suck or were average at best. But this one took me out of my slump.<br/><br/>It was sexy, the plot and story were intriguing. <br/><br/>It's one of the first "wolf" books I've ever read so maybe that's why I was so intrigued. But I was nonetheless.<br/><br/>I can't wait to continue more books in the series!!</span>

<div id="review_1407215762" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1407215762" />
    <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books"><img alt="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528808758p2/37314676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1407215762?book_show_action=true">Oct 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books">NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=paranormal-fantasy-etc">paranormal-fantasy-etc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1407215762" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10944358852479758428"><b>
  <i>***4,5 "Psycho Boy" & "Crazy Bitch" stars from me***</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444476672i/16506766._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Phew... That was intense!!! And beautiful!!! And full of angst!!!<br/>I have to remind you that i read them backward... <br/>I read first "Spiral of need" which was talking about the "Mercury Pack" and because there i met almost everyone in Phoenix Pack, i couldn't resist to learn everything about them...<br/>And i found everything... well, almost... I found out everything about Trey and Taryn and i have to say that i fell in love completely with both of </span>
  <span id="freeText10944358852479758428" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>***4,5 "Psycho Boy" &amp; "Crazy Bitch" stars from me***</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444476672i/16506766._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Phew... That was intense!!! And beautiful!!! And full of angst!!!<br>I have to remind you that i read them backward... <br>I read first "Spiral of need" which was talking about the "Mercury Pack" and because there i met almost everyone in Phoenix Pack, i couldn't resist to learn everything about them...<br>And i found everything... well, almost... I found out everything about Trey and Taryn and i have to say that i fell in love completely with both of them... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444476672ra/16506767.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Even though the one was a little bit psycho and the other a little bit of bitch!!!<br>LOL... They were unbelievably well-fitted together...<br><br>Well, Taryn was forced to mate with a man that she didn't want at all. She was a healer and she was a latent and that wasn't so good for a wolf. Her father wanted to get ride of her and what a great opportunity to give her to someone who will be a wonderfull ally for his pack???<br>One day, Tarryn is waking in a foreign territory and there she is about to discover her fate...<br>The mighty and famous Alpha of the Phoenix Pack, Trey Coleman, is about to make her a deal... <br>But how she can trust this phycho boy??? <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444477252ra/16506831.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Trey when he was fourteen he tried to kill his father and he was banished from his pack and as a teenager he became an Alpha of this one... And beyond that he is a crazy ass who in his wolfish form, he is becoming feral and he can't kill everyone around him...<br><br><b>
  <i>"There had to be something wrong with her if she was attracted to a psycho.<br>But strangely, she didn't feel in danger with him."</i>
</b><br><br>But she can not deny what he is offering her...<br>They will have to pretend that they are mates and from that deal they will earn both of them...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444477252ra/16506832.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Taryn will be out of an unwanted mating and Trey will manage to inform alliances that will stand by him and by his pack when he will deal with his uncle, the Alpha of his old pack.<br><br>From the first moment, Tarryn and Trey are drown to each other and the lust made it unbearable to stay away from each other.<br>But since they have made a deal they can't let themself involved too deep with each other. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391101144ra/8331190.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>They could not be imprinted because the separation after will be unbearable for both of them...<br>But they just can't stay away from each other and they are so cutes together!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419212271ra/13017490.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Okay... Cutes is understatement...<br>They are both dominate wolves and all the time are trying to overpower each other. They don't bow in the other's will...<br>The sex is amazing... It's like a crazy, bloody battle and it was really enjoyable!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444476672ra/16506768.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Not only the sex, but all their interactions was so pleasant to read about them!!!<br>And as the time is passing, it's most difficult for both of them to keep their distances... They are so blind that they can't recognise the truth that it's in front of their eyes...<br><br><b>
  <i>"Love is giving someone the power to completely destroy you, and hoping that they won't..."</i>
</b><br><br>Taryn was a very powerfull little thing...<br>She was tiny in the form and as i said above she is a latent. She can't tranform in her wolfish form, but that doesn't mean that her wolf isn't there all the time!!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444476672i/16506769.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She is very strong and she can overpower everyone like a real Alpha. She is very sarcastic with a big mouth that made me all the time to laugh. Especially when she was interacting with Gretta. <br>And when she was with Trey, she was like a fire... She wanted him from the first moment but she couldn't let herself relax and enjoy what she was living...<br><br>Trey was a very dominant wolf. Everybody feared him. He was the ruler of their world. <br>He was a very serious guy with many responsibilities. He never had fun in his life until the moment Taryn came into his life...<br>His past wasn't good and it had left him big marks in his soul.<br>For the first moment he wanted Taryn but he wanted to dominate her. Something that she could never aloud!<br>He was a very protective and possessive bastard even though Taryn was his contemporary mate.<br>And the strangest thing of all??? Tarryn was the only person in the world that he could calm himself and his wolf down....<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444476672i/16506770.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't say more about them. I'll only say that i loved fiercely Trey and Tarryn. <br>I don't have the words to describe how much and i really liked all the second characters that they surround them... <br>In the beginning the pack was a little bit uncomfortable with Taryn's presence, but very soon, everybody loved her!!!Okay... Not everybody...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444476672i/16506771._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>My only objection on this book was something that happened near to the end... <br>The night of Trey's birthday for all of you that you have read the book!!!<br>No. I'm not a prude or something but that big "scene" bothered me a lot!!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435941753ra/15395346.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>It was like i was seeing different persons from whom i knew in the previous 300 pages...<br>Taryn in whole book wasn't aloud even to Trey to use her, so why she aloud that????<br>And Trey was so damn possesssive with her. Why he aloud it that??? <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402361609ra/9926442.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I just don't understand it and it was like something ugly intruded in my wonderfull bubble and made everything upside down. And after that incident it was everything back to normal...<br>I just don't understand it and i didn't like it and that's why i cut half star from my rating... <br>Because i really loved this book more than "Spiral of need" but that incident frustrated me...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444411127ra/16497363.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, i would like to find out everything for the rest of the guys and i really hope that i won't have more surprises like the one i had here. I don't think that i could bare it!!!<br>And now, i'm just wondering... <br>Will manage someone from the other guys to overstep Trey and Taryn in my heart???<br>I'm not so sure about that!!! I love this couple so damn much!!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444476672i/16506772._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10944358852479758428" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer907291106" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10205170897271296903">The book started off okay but then became annoyingly rapey. With an over the top alpha male who was just boring and a storyline that was blah. Predictable, boring, same-same. If you've read more than a couple of PNRs in your life, then I guarantee you've already read something exactly like this book. Probably even better.</span>

          </span>
        </div>
