  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2915517832" />
    <a title="Erth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35848810-erth"><img alt="Erth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1413992439p2/35848810.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2915517832?book_show_action=true">Aug 02, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erth" href="/user/show/35848810-erth">Erth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2915517832" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14484268496649821631">I really wanted to like this book. I really did. The sample was pretty okay. But man, it's just bad. I can usually consume a romance novel in one afternoon. I can barely read one chapter of this at a time. There's too much exposition. There's so many named characters in each scene that it becomes a parody of 'Too Many Cooks'. The names of said characters are each so unique you find yourself missing the Janes and Johns of the world. But the biggest problem, the most grievous sin, is the main char</span>
  <span id="freeText14484268496649821631" style="display:none">I really wanted to like this book. I really did. The sample was pretty okay. But man, it's just bad. I can usually consume a romance novel in one afternoon. I can barely read one chapter of this at a time. There's too much exposition. There's so many named characters in each scene that it becomes a parody of 'Too Many Cooks'. The names of said characters are each so unique you find yourself missing the Janes and Johns of the world. But the biggest problem, the most grievous sin, is the main character Taryn.<br /><br />She's a foul-mouthed Mary Sue. Her devil-may-care attitude is contrived at best. But worst of all, is her one-liners. She doesn't have conversations. She does vocal drive-bys like Obi-won Kenobi in the Star Wars prequels. Everything is an insult. Everything is a zinger. There aren't any yeses or nopes. She's always at an eleven with "Hell yeah you toad McGee!" or "No ma'am no ham no lambs no Shazam!".<br /><br />It's constant. There's no reprieve. I just want to say goodbye to Taryn. Knowing her, she'd probably say, "Hey daddy-ding-dong, smell ya later! Blammo!".</span>
  <a data-text-id="14484268496649821631" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText4906954770413763645" style="display:none">Quick Review-<b> Mature content reader discretion advised.</b><br>4.5 STARS<br>Genre: Paranormal Romance<br><br><b>
  <i>“Caught. Trapped. And soon to be mounted.”</i>

I was in need of something different so I went back to my roots which is my love for PNR. Feral Sins gave me a good dose of suspense, a touch of mystery with a who done it twist and a very steamy melt your panties romance. I got an alpha male and smart mouthed female that did nothing but turn him on as she rebelled against his need to dominate. She was feisty and he rewarded her feisty ways with a good spank *wink wink* All in all I enjoyed it! <br><br><u>Below is a scene between Trey and Taryn</u><br><br><b>
  <i>Trey smiled wickedly. “When I fuck you Taryn – and make no mistake about it, baby, I will fuck you – the only talking you’ll be doing is begging me to let you come. And don’t doubt that I’ll make you come. Not just the once. You’ll come over and over again, until I decide you’ve had enough. Until I decide that I’ve had enough.”<br>“Hmm. That’s all very fascinating, but you’re forgetting one very important thing.” <br>“And what’s that?” <br>“My guess, Tarzan, is that you’re very used to Janes; you don’t just want total obedience, you expect it. I’m not sure you’d know what to do with a woman who would bite you, scratch you, and curse you to hell and back if she wasn’t getting her own way. You want my submission, you’re going to have to battle for it.”</i>

<span id="freeTextContainer9421940598279874777">Read it the second time :Aug 08, 13<br/><br/><b> FIVE DOMINANT, POSSESSIVE,PREVAILING STARS </b> <br/><br/>Feral Sins (The Phoenix Pack, #1)BY Suzanne Wright <br/><br/>Genres: Paranormal Romance/Erotica/Shapeshifters<br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=saxht0' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688415.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Feral Sins (The Phoenix Pack, #1) is a GREAT book ladies and gentlemen! It is very rare for me to fall in love with <u>everything</u> in a book but this one... The characters, the story, the conversations EVERYTHING!<br/><br/>I read a lot of reviews about this, i got very excited to read this, i had two finals in the past two days a</span>
  <span id="freeText9421940598279874777" style="display:none">Read it the second time :Aug 08, 13<br><br><b> FIVE DOMINANT, POSSESSIVE,PREVAILING STARS </b> <br><br>Feral Sins (The Phoenix Pack, #1)BY Suzanne Wright <br><br>Genres: Paranormal Romance/Erotica/Shapeshifters<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=saxht0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688415.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Feral Sins (The Phoenix Pack, #1) is a GREAT book ladies and gentlemen! It is very rare for me to fall in love with <u>everything</u> in a book but this one... The characters, the story, the conversations EVERYTHING!<br><br>I read a lot of reviews about this, i got very excited to read this, i had two finals in the past two days and i spent the whole time reading it.TOTALLY WORTH IT.- don't worry i did good in the exams.<br><br>This story is about loyalty, control, power, friendship, family, love , and lust.<br><br>I have always been a vampire kind of girl but after reading this i'm gonna get down and dirty with the wolves from now on! ;P<br><br><br>I'm not going to write what this story is about because it will just ruin it for the readers, i -for once didn't read what it was about, i just read the reviews and it seems that everyone fell in love. And it did help that i saw the word <b> Alpha</b>, God this word is awesome! <br>if there is anything that i love more than an Alpha male, it is an Alpha female...<br><br><br> <blockquote>Taryn Warner:</blockquote><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=rc6exl" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412348i/810816._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>: Taryn is one of the greatest characters i have ever read about, she is beautiful and hot in her own way, she doesn't take shit from anyone, she's a badass, but most importantly she is one sarcastic bitch! <br>she really is smart, sarcastic, and an alpha! <br><br><b>
  <blockquote> <i>"I don’t have a submissive bone in my<br>body so don’t bark at me unless you’re happy to be ignored.”</i> </blockquote>
</b><br><br>And everything that comes out of her mouth is plain mean, sexy, or sarcastic , not once i felt that what she said was force and shallow it was natural. Some writers tend to over do the sarcastic and the funny part in their characters and it ends in a disaster.But not this one.<br><br><b> <blockquote><i>“Taryn, are you even listening to me?”<br>“I pretended to, so let that be enough.” <i></i></i></blockquote></b><br><br>And i love her temper and anger, i really love a female with smart comebacks.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<i>“You don’t think that perhaps you have anger management issues?”<br>“Punching people is managing my anger.”</i> </blockquote>
</b><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>No, not forcing myself on them. I’m not a rapist. But I love a challenge, and I love to be in control. Power is a heady thing for me. What great-er power is there than to be able to own someone who doesn't want you someone whose will you can break bit by bit until they have gone from a spirited, dominant, independent individual to a person who is totally submissive to you?”<i> </i></i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>^^^ Lets's just say that things did not end well for this guy. </b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>there were a few ways she could handle her first few moments in their pack. One, she could present them with a dazzling smile and introduce herself needlessly, hoping to win them over with a friendly attitude.Two, she could act aloof, distant, and ignore any attempts to goad her. Or three, she could just be her usual ray of sarcastic fucking sunshine and tell anyone who pushed her to go eat shit.A bigger person would have gone with option two, but, well, she was a bitch. So she decided to go with number three. <i></i></i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>I have a weakness towards the word <b> Alpha</b>. when i see it in a book i say <i> yaaaay </i>. I love the possessiveness and the control that comes with being an alpha.<br><br>And Trey Coleman is not a different. He's the most intense Alpha I've ever read about, maybe because he is an actual Alpha in his pack , but WOo~~HoO swoon worthy character .<br><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=34j7xpd" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412348i/810817._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <blockquote> <i> he was strength and danger and raw sexuality. His presence inside her was like an anchor to her wolf who was a little smug right now, since she was a big fan of psycho boy.</i>
</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Everything that he says is SEX, not really, but that's what it feels like, there are orgasms dripping through his tongue. <br><br><br> <br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>“When I fuck you Taryn – and make no mistake about it, baby, I will fuck you – the only talking you’ll be doing is begging me to let you come. And don’t doubt that I’ll make you come. Not just the once.You’ll come over and over again, until I decide you've had enough. Until I decide that I've had enough.”<br></i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br> <br><br>But he has a sweet, sad, hurt side of him, i really am in love with his character. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"I’m a man which means I’ll fuck up. Regularly. I’m not good with words, I spout crap when I’m angry,and I’m about as romantic as a pebble. But…See, I’m not good with words.All I can say is you’re important to me in a way I can’t explain or understand.More important to me than anything else.”</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>~~~~~<br><br>The relationship between those two is HAWAT!!<br>I don't know if it's a wolf thing, or because they are mates and stuff but EVERYTHING THEY DID AND SAID WAS HOT! <br><br> Here is a bunch of pictures to demonstrate my point ;D<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=35ix6i8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412348ra/810818.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412348i/810820.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=30nkq9u" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412348ra/810821.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Taryn certainly was beneath her anger.<br>Oh not at all! Her wolf wanted to rub against him enticingly, recognizing his scent as the one from the bedroom. Tramp. </i><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2ztha1u" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412348ra/810822.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412348ra/810824.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>~~~~<br><b>SPOILER SCENE </b><br><br><br>There was this scene in the first addition, in Trey's birthday, he does not like birthdays and he never celebrated his , so in order to make him have fun Taryn kind of lures him to have fun by giving him a lot of presents BUT the ultimate gift that makes him change his mind is that she gives him an hour to do with/to her what ever he wants. <br>so after having fun he claims his hour. He brings guys from the pack. to watch and participate, so basically it is an orgy. <br><br>A lot of readers did not like this scene so future readers won't have to read it in other additions. you have to understand that although it is against an alpha wolf to let other touch his mate, but in this scene i found it totally cool, i mean he wanted to proof that she was his, and he's the only one who is going to touch fuck and see her,and only if HE decide other wise then she's his. And here he let the guy touch her and see him doing her. <br>Before Taryn came to the pack they did this more than once, so i guess it was normal for them, the guys loved her, and respected her so for me this scene was not weird or anything it was hot, sexy, erotic, and FUN. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=saxht0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688415.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Warning: This novel contains an extremely sarcastic Alpha female, a broody possessive Alpha male, bitter in-laws, voyeuristic enforcers, a whole lot of dirty talk, and steamy bedroom battles for dominance. Reader Advisory: This book also contains a graphic ménage scene - not for the faint-hearted.</i><br><br><br><br> </span>

    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1146455964?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1146455964" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12597068417034654028"><b>You’re safe with me."</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427690475i/14307207.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If you are a fan of paranormal romance than Feral Sins is the read for you!<br/><br/>Taryn is what is known in the wolf world as a latent wolf. She is also the healer of her pack and the daughter of the alpha of her pack. Taryn's father has decided she should mate an alpha-ass named Roscoe from another pack in order to join the two packs together. Taryn is an independent woman and is not at all excited about her Dad's plan for her life. <br/><br/>Trey is an alpha wool from the Phoenix Pack. He </span>
  <span id="freeText12597068417034654028" style="display:none"><b>You’re safe with me."</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427690475i/14307207.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you are a fan of paranormal romance than Feral Sins is the read for you!<br><br>Taryn is what is known in the wolf world as a latent wolf. She is also the healer of her pack and the daughter of the alpha of her pack. Taryn's father has decided she should mate an alpha-ass named Roscoe from another pack in order to join the two packs together. Taryn is an independent woman and is not at all excited about her Dad's plan for her life. <br><br>Trey is an alpha wool from the Phoenix Pack. He has been challenged by his uncle. HIs pack is at stake. Trey decides to present Taryn with a deal. <br><br> <b>“I need alliances, Taryn. Your dad collects them like they’re coupons. If I had an alliance with him, I would have a link to his alliances and then I’d have plenty of wolves to call on for this battle. Maybe it will make my uncle hesitate, maybe it won’t. In any case, the situation will be evened out.”-Trey</b><br><br>Easy deal! All Taryn has to do is mate with Trey and then she can get away from her father and Roscoe! She agrees to the deal and they make a plan!<br><br>It isn't hard for Trey to claim Taryn. Once a wolf "claims" his mate no one can interfere with the bond. Taryn and Trey must form their bond intimately in order for everyone to believe that they are truly mated. They don't have any problems consummating the relationship. Together these two are super steamy! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427690475i/14307208.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As Trey and Taryn's bond begins to grow. Trey gets spooked and begins to pull away from Taryn emotionally. As she has already started to truly bond with him, it is painful and heart breaking.<br> <br><b>"Trey doesn’t count in an emotional sense, but I still didn’t expect this feeling of being… trapped. I’m bound to someone who won’t even touch me socially, who deliberately avoids me— unless I want to be left alone."-Taryn </b><br><br>Taryn has bonded with the wolfs from Trey's pack. It takes some time for Trey to get his head together. <br><br><b>"One thing was for sure— she was a better person than he would ever be. She was someone who any male would be proud to have as his mate, temporary or not."-Trey</b><br><br>When Trey finally realizes his feelings for Taryn, he decides he wants her to stay. It's hard for Taryn to accept that he truly wants to be with her.<br><br><b>“It’s okay, baby. You’re safe, I swear. It’s okay.”-Trey</b><br><br>They are a true match and together everything makes sense. <br><br><b>"She loved Trey Coleman. The realization punched the breath from her lungs."-Taryn</b><br><br>Let's just say when an alpha wolf makes up his mind there is no changing it!<br><br><b>“All I know is that I don’t want you to leave. If you do, I’ll hunt you down and bring you back , Taryn, I shit you not, I will. Not because of our deal or my wolf , but because I want you here with me.”-Trey</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427690475i/14307211.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although finally together, they have so many obstacles to over come. Will Trey be able to overthrow his uncle? Will Taryn's family every truly accept Trey as her mate? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427690475i/14307209.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>“Love is giving someone the power to completely destroy you , and hoping that they won’t.” </b><br><br>Feral Sins kept me up all night long! I was so drawn into the story I had to see what would happen next. Taryn is a strong heroine that stands up for herself. She is funny and strong! Trey is a damaged hero that is afraid to love.<br><br><b>"He hadn’t thought of his life as something that was dark or empty until she came here and suddenly lit it up and filled it."-Trey </b><br><br>Together they make a power couple like no other. I highly recommend this book to anyone who likes paranormal romance! There is a well developed plot line, humor, action, and of course lots of steam! You will not be disappointed!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427690475i/14307210.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer628309479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13590515738069278102"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*I love Trey, I do*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <u>Fifth re-read: 02.11.18</u>
</b><br/>I made a review for the fifth re-read only for it to get deleted. Typical. Anyways, the book centers around the latent female wolf shifter and a healer (she can heal the actual wounds within minutes, guaranteeing a recovery) <b>Taryn Warner</b> (23? 24? 25?) and alpha male wolf shifter with a dangerous reputation <b>Trey ‘psycho boy’ ‘Flinstone’ Coleman</b> (how old?). The story starts with Taryn and Trey making a deal; pretend to be true mates. Tr</span>
  <span id="freeText13590515738069278102" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*I love Trey, I do*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Fifth re-read: 02.11.18</u>
</b><br>I made a review for the fifth re-read only for it to get deleted. Typical. Anyways, the book centers around the latent female wolf shifter and a healer (she can heal the actual wounds within minutes, guaranteeing a recovery) <b>Taryn Warner</b> (23? 24? 25?) and alpha male wolf shifter with a dangerous reputation <b>Trey ‘psycho boy’ ‘Flinstone’ Coleman</b> (how old?). The story starts with Taryn and Trey making a deal; pretend to be true mates. Trey needs alliances that Taryn's father can give him, and Taryn needs to get away for a arranged mating done by her father. However, neither expected to care for each other or how strongly their wolves react towards one another. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Just give me a second. Attempting to give a fuck...Attempting harder to give a fuck...Sorry, there was an error; fuck not given.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Overall, I adore this book. <b>I still wish we had gotten one more book that centers around Trey and Taryn</b>. Though my rating is technically less, I refuse to change it simply because I refuse to believe it's still not a good as it used to be. So the rating stays the same.... It's not the books fault that I'm mostly numb for the past year or so. Trey is still one of my favorite characters and that will never change. Taryn is still funny as hell and together they are awesome. I kinda want to demand a second book for these two, though I know that it'll never happen. <b>Also, I'm not interested in reading the rest of the series</b> after the COMPLETE bust book number two was. I hated it.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Wouldn’t you like to slip into something more comfortable though? Perhaps a coma?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Other characters</u>:</b><br>→ <b>Roscoe Weston</b>, an sleazy Alpha wolf who wants to mate Taryn to make her submit to him. This he does by making a deal with her father; an alliance. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Trey kills him. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Dante ‘Mountain Man’</b>, Trey's Beta.<br>→ <b>Tao</b>, Trey's Head Enforcer, becomes Taryn’s personal bodyguard.<br>→ <b>Dominic ‘Dom’ ‘Blondie?’</b>, one of Trey's enforcers.<br>→ <b>Ryan ‘Grumpy’</b>, one of Trey's enforcers.<br>→ <b>Marcus ‘Smiley’</b>, one of Trey's enforcers. <br>→ <b>Patrick ‘Trick’ ‘Burly’</b>, one of Trey's enforcers. Trick and Marcus are best friend and scratches each others inch now and then. <br>→ <b>Greta Tyler</b>, Trey's grandmother.<br>→ <b>Grace</b>, a packmate of Phoenix Pack. Her mate, <b>Rhett</b><br>→ <b>Brock</b>, a cousin of Trey’s dad and packmate of Phoenix Pack. <b>Kirk</b>, Brock’s son, so he’s sort of Trey’s cousin. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Brock's the traitor; gets executed. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Cam</b> and his mate, <b>Lydia</b>, packmates of Phoenix Pack.<br>→ <b>Selma</b> and <b>Hope</b>, the Barbies, packmates of Phoenix Pack.<br>→ <b>Joseph ‘Joey’ Winters,</b>, Taryn's dead true mate. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[After meeting Trey, it was proven that Joey was not Taryn's true mate after all. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Summer</b>, Trey's dead true mate. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[After meeting Taryn, it was proven that Summer was not Trey's true mate after all.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <b>Viv</b>, Summer’s mom.<br>→ <b>Shaya Critchley</b> (23) and <b>Caleb</b>, Taryn's two best friends.<br>→ <b>Lance Kai Warner</b> (43), Alpha and Taryn's father. Only cares about his image. His bodyguard, <b>Zack</b>.<br>→ <b>Oscar</b> and <b>Perry</b>, Lance's enforcers.<br>→ <b>Brodie</b>, a female wolf who hates Taryn. Part of Lance's pack.<br>→ <b>Darryl Coleman</b>, Alpha of the Bjorn Pack, Trey's uncle who wants to unite both pack with him as Alpha. He has a perverse wish to see Trey bow down to him. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Trey kills him at the end of the book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Don</b>, Taryn's uncle.<br>→ <b>Nick Axton</b>, the Alpha of the Ryland Pack, Don's pack. His Beta, <b>Jon</b>.<br>→ <b>Derren</b>, Nick's bodyguard.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Taryn, are you even listening to me?<br>“I pretended to, so let that be enough” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Paranormal Romance.<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book One. <br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Trey Coleman.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Just the first one, I couldn't stand book #2.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Probably.<br><b>Rating</b> - 5 (though truth be told it's less; I just refuse to admit it) stars.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Fourth re-read: 13.08.16</u>
</b><br>Yep, I was right: I read it yet again. God, I cannot get enough of this book! I really, really hope-need-pray-beg that <b>
  <i>Suzanne Wright</i>
</b> writes another book with Trey and Taryn as main characters. I really do.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Third re-read: 09.10.15</u>
</b><br>Still fucking perfect! 100% sure that I'll re-read it yet again soon.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 11.03.15</u>
</b><br>Can't go long without my 'Trey' fix. He's like my addiction.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 28.03.14</u>
</b><br>Even better than the first time. What can I say: Trey does that to you. You cannot help but to love him. Need him. Obsessed about him... Already I need him again.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424716034i/13794879.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This is where I’ll be very, very soon, Taryn,” he promised – more like threatened. “Inside you, filling you with my cum, and making you scream.”<br>“I’ve met guys like you before. They talk the talk but, well…talking doesn’t exactly get people to orgasm, does it?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396042335ra/9081706.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m going to fuck you hard and deep now, Taryn. Fuck you until you’re dripping with my cum. And you’re going to take it like a good girl.”<br>“You cock-smoking shitfaced motherfucking piece of monkey shit,” she growled.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396043268ra/9081881.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>For those who hasn't read this amazing book, are seriously missing out on the most incredible journey. <b>The characters are simply perfect</b> and the story is strong and never boring. You get completely dragged into the book, like the rest of the world disappears and it's only you and Suzanne Wright's world there. The story shows how, even though people keep pushing you down, keep trying to break you, you still have to fight. <b>Fight for the chance of happiness</b>, that there is something good out there for you. I, for one, felt extremely sorrow for Taryn, and how her own father/his pack treated her. That they made her put up so strong walls around her, not letting anyone in, it was sad to read. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“She's one of those people who are like Slinkies.”<br>“Slinkies?”<br>“Yeah. Basically useless, but they make you smile when you push them down the stairs.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Though, because of all that, <b>I felt myself look up at Taryn like a role model</b>. Her snarky, snappy comments and her spirit was just amazing and inspiring. I love how she slowly was able to get dominate alpha Trey to open up. To have some fun. Fun he never get to have. I remember first time reading this book, that Trey's story got me eyes wet. And it still does. I love how two broken souls come together and become one hell of a team. I recommend this book for pretty much everyone, and if you don't like it then you live in 'La La Land' as Taryn would say :) <br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396041422ra/9081482.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re all there is for me, Taryn. I’m broken baby. You know that. Before you… it was like those bits of me were just scattered all over the place. I’ve never felt whole. Not until you. You hold those pieces together. It’s not an exaggeration when I say you hold my sanity in your hands. Without you, I’d fall apart.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396042090ra/9081653.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Love is giving someone the power to completely destroy you, and hoping that they won’t” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396042221ra/9081686.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When I fuck you Taryn – and make no mistake about it, baby, I will fuck you – the only talking you’ll be doing is begging me to let you come. And don’t doubt that I’ll make you come. Not just the once. You’ll come over and over again, until I decide you’ve had enough. Until I decide that I’ve had enough.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396041422ra/9081483.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I like it when you’re out of control.”<br>“Not like this, baby, you don’t want me like this. Tell me to ease off.”<br>“Why would I do that? I don’t want you being someone you’re not.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380438062i/885506.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I want so badly another book for Trey and Taryn with they kid <b>Kye River Coleman</b> How Kye is, how Trey is with Kye, how Taryn is as a mother... I WANT MORE! And boy, I want to see Kye grow up and become an Alpha and Trey being all proud!!!! GIVE ME PLEASE!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444412852ra/16497508.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Rate: 5 stars.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HHSFCz2R6U5rTi8UKj1UkuuY+3UiJv1x5GtUE+KaxuW6IzPTFGsvI3d8BZioyWjQIJk9Z+3fSLdXSgyrF4OWiA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('04xeaRrSONKOGq/OAvvHxfdSYJXzid1bRhvN8bshuDR12+ixMyj+v5IohUKAD/uHPFOmhzxwaJ31OpVJTjjoWQ==')})
  }
